The Company Overview Presentation includes a discussion of\nthe Company\x92s historical operating results using various non-GAAP financial\nmeasures, including (i)\xa0earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation and\namortization (EBITDA)\xa0and (ii)\xa0cash, cash equivalents and short-term\ninvestments, excluding short-term borrowings, long-term borrowings and\nconvertible subordinated debentures (Net Cash). A \x93non-GAAP financial measure\x94\nis defined as a numerical measure of a company\x92s performance that excludes or\nincludes amounts so as to be different than the most directly comparable\nmeasure calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted\naccounting principles (\x93GAAP\x94). Pursuant to the requirements of Regulation\xa0G,\nthe Company has included a reconciliation of all non-GAAP financial measures in\nthe Company Overview Presentation, and has posted this information on the\nCompany\x92s website at http://www.aspect.com/ir/index.cfm.\n\n\n', u'\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0\xa0Management of the Company uses EBITDA in monitoring and evaluating the\nCompany\x92s ongoing financial results and trends excluding these items.\nManagement uses Net Cash to analyze the Company\x92s total cash position minus\ntotal debt position, which provides insight into usable cash (free of\nencumbrance). Management believes that viewing this usable cash position is\nneeded from a cash use planning perspective. Management believes that analysis\nof each of EBITDA and Net Cash provides important insights into the Company\x92s\noperating results and trends and impacts future planning. We believe that\ninvestors should have the benefit of viewing the presentation in the same\nmanner as management does in running our business operations.
